: 05-10-2023 15:41:16: = SELECT MAS_LEADS_TRANS.*, MAS_REASON.* , CALL_SEARCH_CITY.* , MAS_RESON_DENY.* FROM MAS_LEADS_TRANS 
 LEFT JOIN MAS_REASON   ON   MAS_LEADS_TRANS.RES_CODE =MAS_REASON.RES_CODE
  LEFT JOIN CALL_SEARCH_CITY  ON MAS_LEADS_TRANS.CITY_NAME_T  = CALL_SEARCH_CITY.CITY_CODE
   LEFT JOIN MAS_RESON_DENY   ON MAS_LEADS_TRANS.RES_CODE  = MAS_RESON_DENY.RES_CODE
 WHERE ANUMBER = :ANUMBER AND AGENT_ID = :AGENT_ID  AND MAS_REASON.RES_NAME = :RES_NAME AND CALL_SEARCH_CITY.CITY_CODE
 = MAS_LEADS_TRANS.CITY_NAME_T

  LEFT JOIN CALL_SEARCH_CITY  ON MAS_LEADS_TRANS.CITY_NAME_T  = CALL_SEARCH_CITY.CITY_CODE
   LEFT JOIN MAS_RESON_DENY   ON MAS_LEADS_TRANS.RES_CODE  = MAS_RESON_DENY.RES_CODE
